<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">трой-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">troj-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тройка.html>тро́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тройка.html>тро́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тройка.html>тро́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тройка.html>тро́ек</a></b>)

***тронуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нуть</a> (3063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trónutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch</li>
<li>to move <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">emotionally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to bother, to annoy, to disturb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start moving</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to damage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of frost</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуться.html>тро́нуться</a> (4549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a> (9846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тропа.html>тро́п</a>(ик)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tróp(ik)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tropíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tropical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:климат.html>кли́мат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tropíčeskij</b> klímat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tropical climate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tropíčeskij</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">torrid zone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадка.html>лихора́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tropíčeskaja</b> lixorádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jungle fever, dengue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tropíčeskij</b> les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rainforest, hylea</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тростник.html>тростни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trostník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тростник.html>тростника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тростник.html>тростники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тростник.html>тростнико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reed, rush (grass-like plant)</li></ol>

***трофейный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трофейный.html>трофе́йный</a> (8852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трофей.html>трофе́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">troféj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трофейный.html>трофе́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">troféjnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>trophy, captured
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трофейный.html>трофе́йная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>troféjnaja</b> puška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">captured gun</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трофейный.html>трофе́йные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:произведение.html>произведе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>troféjnyje</b> proizvedénija iskússtva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trophy art (works)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***троюродный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a> (18208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tróje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ю-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ju-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ю-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ju-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by analogy with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see there for further details).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trojúrodnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">denotes a relative in the same generation as the head noun but two degrees greater in separation</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>брат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trojúrodnyj brat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male second cousin, brother’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:племянник.html>племя́нник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trojúrodnyj plemjánnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male second cousin once removed, nephew’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внук.html>внук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trojúrodnyj vnuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male first cousin twice removed, grandson’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правнук.html>пра́внук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trojúrodnyj právnuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male first cousin three times removed, great-grandson’s generation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>There is no single equivalent of this term in English. It is applied to close relations (e.g. brothers, uncles, grandfathers) and indicates a relation that is in the same generation as the term being modified, but is two degrees greater in separation in terms of the closest common ancestor. For example, the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a></span> equivalent of one's brother is one's second cousin, because one has a common father with one's brother, but a common great-grandfather with one's second cousin. (Logically, to find the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a></span> equivalent of a given relation, find the nearest common ancestor, go two generations up, and then go two generations back down, following different children.) See the table at <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for more information.</li></ul>

***труба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a> (1077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">truba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*trǫba</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trubá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>трубы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>тру́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pipe</li>
<li>chimney, flue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trumpet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> undesirable situation, seemingly hopeless (<a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mobile phone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial, figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> telephone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hunters' lingo<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fox tail</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубач.html>труба́ч</a> (10749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Formally can be from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trubá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, semantically from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trubítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубач.html>труба́ч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trubáč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубач.html>трубача́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубач.html>трубачи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубач.html>трубаче́й</a></b>)
</p>

***трубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a> (14023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протрубить.html>протруби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow <i>(the trumpet)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>трубу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trubítʹ</b> v trubú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trumpet; blow/sound the trumpet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trubítʹ</b> v rog</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blow the horn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sound, to blare
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>трубы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>трубя́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">truby <b>trubját</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">trumpets sound/blare</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sound <i>(a signal)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trubítʹ</b> trevógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sound the alarm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trubítʹ</b> sbor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sound the assembly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to trumpet, to proclaim from the housetops
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трубить.html>труби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trubítʹ</b> vo vse úši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to din into the ears</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бка</a> (690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trubá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trúbka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tube, small pipe</li>
<li>roll, scroll</li>
<li>telephone receiver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубка.html>тру́бку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ trúbku, bratʹ trúbku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to answer incoming call</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tobacco pipe</li>
<li>snorkel</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trubá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чист</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čist</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to clean, to scour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
